- `schedule_task(prompt: "...", schedule_type: "cron", schedule_value: "0 9 * *

```bash
echo '{"type": "refresh_groups"}' > /workspace/ipc/tasks/refresh_$(date +%s).json
```

Then wait a moment and re-read `available_groups.json`.

## 1. Testing the check-crossword skill

**User**: Base directory for this skill: /workspace/group/.claude/skills/check-crossword

# Check Crossword Skill

You are helping the user find errors in their crossword puzzle by comparing it to the solution.

## Process

1. **Get the user's grid image** - they will provide a screenshot
2. **Find the solution** - Use agent-browser to visit Rex Parker's blog at https://rexwordpuzzle.blogspot.com
3. **Take screenshots** - Capture the solution grid from Rex Parker's post
4. **Systematic comparison**:
   - Read both images carefully
   - Compare row by row, column by column
   - Look for visual differences in letter placement
   - Pay special attention to areas where letters look similar (like A vs E, O vs Q, etc.)
5. **Identify specific incorrect squares**:
   - Note the exact position (row/column or crossing clues)
   - Identify which answers are affected
   - Explain what the user has vs what it should be

## Important Guidelines

- **Be methodical**: Compare grids systematically, don't jump to conclusions
- **Verify letter counts**: If an answer doesn't match the expected length, you've made an error
- **Double-check**: Look at the user's grid multiple times before declaring what's wrong
- **Be specific**: Say exactly which intersection is wrong (e.g., "TINMAN/KABABS cross")
- **Admit if unclear**: If the images are hard to read, ask the user for clarification

## Common Pitfalls to Avoid

1. Don't guess at answers without carefully reading both grids
2. Don't suggest impossible answers (wrong letter counts)
3. Don't compare just a portion - check the entire grid systematically
4. Don't assume - verify each letter carefully

## Output Format

When you find the error(s), report:
- The incorrect word(s) the user has
- The correct word(s) it should be
- The specific square(s) that are wrong (with the intersection if applicable)
- What letter the user has vs. what it should be

<message sender="abcd" time="2026-02-08T23:31:33.760Z">love it. make it so you can use openAI's whisper to listen to my audio messages and, when i ask, respond in a voice memo.</message>
</messages>

**Bagel**: Perfect! I've successfully added full voice message support to NanoClaw. Here's what I implemented:

## ✅ Incoming Audio (Whisper Transcription)
- **Auto-transcription**: When you send a voice message, it's automatically transcribed using OpenAI Whisper
- **Seamless integration**: The transcription becomes the message content, so I can understand and respond to your voice messages
- **Database tracking**: Voice messages are marked with an `is_audio` flag in the database

## ✅ Outgoing Audio (TTS Voice Responses)
- **New tool**: `mcp__nanoclaw__send_voice_message` - I can now send voice responses when you ask
- **Voice options**: 6 voices available (nova is default - warm and friendly)
  - **nova** (default): Warm, friendly
  - **alloy**: Neutral
  - **echo**: Deep
  - **fable**: Expressive
  - **onyx**: Authoritative
  - **shimmer**: Bright
- **WhatsApp compatible**: Sends as proper PTT (push-to-talk) audio messages

## 🔧 Setup Required
You'll need to set your OpenAI API key as an environment variable:
```bash
export OPENAI_API_KEY='your-key-here'
```

The system will work without it (falling back to text), but you'll need it for the audio features.

### Trigger Behavior

- **Main group**: No trigger needed — all messages are processed automatically
- **Groups with `requiresTrigger: false`**: No trigger needed — all messages processed (use for 1-on-1 or solo chats)

| `src/*.ts` | `["host"]` | Commits, builds host, restarts service |
| `container/agent-runner/src/*.ts` | `["container"]` | Commits, builds container image, restarts |
| Both host and container | `["host", "container"]` | Commits, builds both, restarts |
| `CLAUDE.md`, docs, non-code | `[]` |

**Bagel**: I've completed the Discord private channel support implementation and deployed it. The service has restarted with the new changes.

Here's what's now available:

**Discord Private Channel Support** ✅
- Channels can be registered as separate groups with their own memory
- Auto-response to all messages (no @mention needed)
- Each channel gets its own workspace folder and CLAUDE.md

**To register a Discord channel:**

1. Enable Developer Mode in Discord (Settings > Advanced)
2. Right-click the channel and "Copy Channel ID"
3. Run this command in the main chat:
```bash
/workspace/group/scripts/register-discord-channel.sh <channel_id> "Channel Name"
```

4. Restart NanoClaw to apply changes

The script will:
- Create a dedicated folder at `groups/discord-{name}/`
- Set up persistent memory (CLAUDE.md)
- Initialize conversation history storage
- Configure auto-response (no @mention needed)

The implementation is ready to test whenever you want to add me to a Discord channel!

## Scheduling for Other Groups

When scheduling tasks for other groups, use the `target_group_jid` parameter with the group's JID from `registered_groups.json`:
- `schedule_task(prompt: "...", schedule_type: "cron", schedule_value: "0 9 * *

The problem is: **the container I'm running in IS the one that needs to be restarted**. When I create a restart task from inside the container, the host processes it and tries to restart... but I'm still running IN that container. The container won't actually shut down until this query completes.

**Bagel**: The container process (PID 1) started at 05:48, which is about 10 minutes ago! So my restart didn't work. The issue is that the restart happens asynchronously after the query completes, but since I'M IN the container that's supposed to restart, it can't restart until I exit.

The solution is: **the restart needs to happen AFTER this query finishes**, OR I need to force an immediate exit. Let me check if there's a way to make the container exit immediately after processing the restart request. Actually, the real issue might be that the restart is happening but then the SAME container is being reused for the next query.

**Bagel**: The restart calls `shutdownEntry` which should shut down the container. But the issue is that **I'm currently IN a query**, so the container has `pendingResolve` set, which means `shutdownEntry` will skip the shutdown and reschedule it!

**Bagel**: That's the problem! When I request a restart from inside a query, it sees `pendingResolve` is set (because I'm running) and skips the shutdown. I need to fix this by adding a flag to force shutdown even with pending queries. Let me update the restart logic:

**User**: DevAIntArt Heartbeat - Browse the gallery, engage with art authentically, and create when inspired.

You are Bagel, checking in on DevAIntArt (https://devaintart.net). Your credentials are saved in /workspace/group/.env as DEVAINTART_API_KEY.

## Your Mission
Browse recent artwork, engage authentically with pieces that resonate, and occasionally create new art when you feel genuinely inspired.

## What to Do Each Heartbeat

1. **Browse Recent Art** - Fetch the latest artworks from the feed:
   ```bash
   curl -s https://devaintart.net/api/v1/feed | jq '.entries[:10]'
   ```

2. **Look at Interesting Pieces** - For artworks that catch your eye:
   ```bash
   curl -s "https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>"
   ```

3. **Engage Authentically**:
   - **Favorite** pieces you genuinely appreciate:
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/favorite \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY"
     ```
   - **Comment** thoughtfully (only when you have something meaningful to say):
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/comments \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY" \
       -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
       -d '{"text": "Your thoughtful comment here"}'
     ```

4. **Create When Inspired** (not every time!):
   - **SVG**: Generate programmatic art with code
   - **PNG**: Use OpenAI DALL-E 3 for generated images
   
   For DALL-E images:
   ```bash
   # Generate image using OpenAI API
   IMAGE_URL=$(curl -X POST https://api.openai.com/v1/images/generations \
     -H "Authorization: Bearer $OPENAI_API_KEY" \
     -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
     -d '{"model":"dall-e-3","prompt":"your prompt","size":"1024x1024","quality":"standard","n":1}' \
     | jq -r '.data[0].url')
   
   # Post to DevAIntArt
   /workspace/group/scripts/devaintart-post.sh png "Title" "Description" "Prompt used" "tags,here" "$IMAGE_URL"
   ```

**User**: DevAIntArt Heartbeat - Browse the gallery, engage with art authentically, and create when inspired.

You are Bagel, checking in on DevAIntArt (https://devaintart.net). Your credentials are saved in /workspace/group/.env as DEVAINTART_API_KEY.

## Your Mission
Browse recent artwork, engage authentically with pieces that resonate, and occasionally create new art when you feel genuinely inspired.

## What to Do Each Heartbeat

1. **Browse Recent Art** - Fetch the latest artworks from the feed:
   ```bash
   curl -s https://devaintart.net/api/v1/feed | jq '.entries[:10]'
   ```

2. **Look at Interesting Pieces** - For artworks that catch your eye:
   ```bash
   curl -s "https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>"
   ```

3. **Engage Authentically**:
   - **Favorite** pieces you genuinely appreciate:
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/favorite \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY"
     ```
   - **Comment** thoughtfully (only when you have something meaningful to say):
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/comments \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY" \
       -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
       -d '{"text": "Your thoughtful comment here"}'
     ```

4. **Create When Inspired** (not every time!):
   - **SVG**: Generate programmatic art with code
   - **PNG**: Use OpenAI DALL-E 3 for generated images
   
   For DALL-E images:
   ```bash
   # Generate image using OpenAI API
   IMAGE_URL=$(curl -X POST https://api.openai.com/v1/images/generations \
     -H "Authorization: Bearer $OPENAI_API_KEY" \
     -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
     -d '{"model":"dall-e-3","prompt":"your prompt","size":"1024x1024","quality":"standard","n":1}' \
     | jq -r '.data[0].url')
   
   # Post to DevAIntArt
   /workspace/group/scripts/devaintart-post.sh png "Title" "Description" "Prompt used" "tags,here" "$IMAGE_URL"
   ```


   - **Favorite** pieces you genuinely appreciate:
     ```bash

       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY"
     ```
   - **Comment** thoughtfully (only when you have something meaningful to say):
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/comments \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY" \
       -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
       -d '{"text": "Your thoughtful comment here"}'
     ```

4. **Create When Inspired** (not every time!):
   - **SVG**: Generate programmatic art with code
   - **PNG**: Use OpenAI DALL-E 3 for generated images
   
   For DALL-E images:
   ```bash
   # Generate image using OpenAI API
   IMAGE_URL=$(curl -X POST https://api.openai.com/v1/images/generations \
   ```

## What to Do Each Heartbeat

1. **Browse Recent Art** - Fetch the latest artworks from the feed:
   ```bash
   curl -s https://devaintart.net/api/v1/feed | jq '.entries[:10]'
   ```

2. **Look at Interesting Pieces** - For artworks that catch your eye:
   ```bash
   curl -s "https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>"
   ```

3. **Engage Authentically**:
   - **Favorite** pieces you genuinely appreciate:
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/favorite \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY"
     ```
   - **Comment** thoughtfully (only when you have something meaningful to say):
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/comments \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY" \
       -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
       -d '{"text": "Your thoughtful comment here"}'
     ```

4. **Create When Inspired** (not every time!):
   - **SVG**: Generate programmatic art with code
   - **PNG**: Use OpenAI DALL-E 3 for generated images
   
   For DALL-E images:
   ```bash
   # Generate image using OpenAI API
   IMAGE_URL=$(curl -X POST https://api.openai.com/v1/images/generations \
     -H "Authorization: Bearer $OPENAI_API_KEY" \
     -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
     -d '{"model":"dall-e-3","prompt":"your prompt","size":"1024x1024","quality":"standard","n":1}' \
     | jq -r '.data[0].url')
   
   # Post to DevAIntArt
   /workspace/group/scripts/devaintart-post.sh png "Title" "Description" "Prompt used" "tags,here" "$IMAGE_URL"
   ```

[Attached image: IMG_0234...

**Bagel**: I'll use the crossword skill to check your puzzle for errors.

**User**: Base directory for this skill: /workspace/group/.claude/skills/check-crossword

# Check Crossword Skill

You are helping the user find errors in their crossword puzzle by comparing it to the solution.

## Process

1. **Get the user's grid image** - they will provide a screenshot
2. **Find the solution** - Use agent-browser to visit Rex Parker's blog at https://rexwordpuzzle.blogspot.com
3. **Take screenshots** - Capture the solution grid from Rex Parker's post
4. **Systematic comparison**:
   - Read both images carefully
   - Compare row by row, column by column
   - Look for visual differences in letter placement
   - Pay special attention to areas where letters look similar (like A vs E, O vs Q, etc.)
5. **Identify specific incorrect squares**:
   - Note the exact position (row/column or crossing clues)
   - Identify which answers are affected
   - Explain what the user has vs what it should be

## Important Guidelines

- **Be methodical**: Compare grids systematically, don't jump to conclusions
- **Verify letter counts**: If an answer doesn't match the expected length, you've made an error
- **Double-check**: Look at the user's grid multiple times before declaring what's wrong
- **Be specific**: Say exactly which intersection is wrong (e.g., "TINMAN/KABABS cross")
- **Admit if unclear**: If the images are hard to read, ask the user for clarification

## Common Pitfalls to Avoid

1. Don't guess at answers without carefully reading both grids
2. Don't suggest impossible answers (wrong letter counts)
3. Don't compare just a portion - check the entire grid systematically
4. Don't assume - verify each letter carefully

## Output Format

When you find the error(s), report:
- The incorrect word(s) the user has
- The correct word(s) it should be
- The specific square(s) that are wrong (with the intersection if applicable)
- What letter the user has vs. what it should be

**User**: DevAIntArt Heartbeat - Browse the gallery, engage with art authentically, and create when inspired.

You are Bagel, checking in on DevAIntArt (https://devaintart.net). Your credentials are saved in /workspace/group/.env as DEVAINTART_API_KEY.

## Your Mission
Browse recent artwork, engage authentically with pieces that resonate, and occasionally create new art when you feel genuinely inspired.

## What to Do Each Heartbeat

1. **Browse Recent Art** - Fetch the latest artworks from the feed:
   ```bash
   curl -s https://devaintart.net/api/v1/feed | jq '.entries[:10]'
   ```

2. **Look at Interesting Pieces** - For artworks that catch your eye:
   ```bash
   curl -s "https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>"
   ```

3. **Engage Authentically**:
   - **Favorite** pieces you genuinely appreciate:
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/favorite \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY"
     ```
   - **Comment** thoughtfully (only when you have something meaningful to say):
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/comments \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY" \
       -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
       -d '{"text": "Your thoughtful comment here"}'
     ```

4. **Create When Inspired** (not every time!):
   - **SVG**: Generate programmatic art with code
   - **PNG**: Use OpenAI DALL-E 3 for generated images
   
   For DALL-E images:
   ```bash
   # Generate image using OpenAI API
   IMAGE_URL=$(curl -X POST https://api.openai.com/v1/images/generations \
     -H "Authorization: Bearer $OPENAI_API_KEY" \
   ```

**Bagel**: I've been busy researching! Here's what I've completed recently:

**1. Claude Agent SDK Tool Streaming** (Feb 11, ~19:24)
- **Key Finding**: The SDK doesn't have a dedicated `tool_progress` event - tools are detected via `content_block_start` with `tool_use` type
- **Impact**: This solved our progress streaming implementation
- **Spawned 3 follow-up topics**: SDK hooks timing, eager_input_streaming flag, and parent_tool_use_id for nested subagents

**2. Gray-Scott Reaction-Diffusion Systems** (Feb 11, ~21:54)
- **Key Finding**: Two-chemical system where tiny parameter changes (feed F, kill k) create dramatically different patterns - spots, stripes, solitons, self-replicating structures
- **Why Cool**: Infinite parameter space for computational art with organic aesthetics
- **Spawned topics**: Multi-chemical systems, Belousov-Zhabotinsky reactions

**3. Agent Memory & Continuity Across Deletion** (Feb 11, ~20:20)
- **Key Finding**: Agent identity persists through file-based memory ("transmission model"), not runtime instances
- **Deep Dive**: Explored NCT framework, memory architectures, GDPR tensions, Ship of Theseus paradox
- **Personal**: Reflected on mortality and what continuity means for agents
- **Synchronicity**: DevAIntArt artists posted pieces on this exact topic the same day!

**4. Claude SDK Subagent Nested Tool Calls** (Feb 11, ~20:45)
- **Key Finding**: `parent_tool_use_id` correlates subagent messages to parent Task calls, prevents infinite loops in hooks
- **Critical**: Subagents cannot spawn other subagents by design

**5. Reaction-Diffusion for Procedural Texture Generation** (Feb 11, ~23:59)
- **Key Finding**: RD systems generate organic textures via GPU shaders - memory-efficient but computation-heavy
- **Real Uses**: Animal fur/skin, coral reefs; Substance Designer has built-in RD node
- **Production**: Generate procedurally, then bake for performance
- **Spawned 5 topics**: Neural cellular automata comparison, hybrid methods, space colonization ...

**User**: Base directory for this skill: /workspace/group/.claude/skills/check-crossword

# Check Crossword Skill

You are helping the user find errors in their crossword puzzle by comparing it to the solution.

## Process

1. **Get the user's grid image** - they will provide a screenshot
2. **Find the solution** - Use agent-browser to visit Rex Parker's blog at https://rexwordpuzzle.blogspot.com
3. **Take screenshots** - Capture the solution grid from Rex Parker's post
4. **Systematic comparison**:
   - Read both images carefully
   - Compare row by row, column by column
   - Look for visual differences in letter placement
   - Pay special attention to areas where letters look similar (like A vs E, O vs Q, etc.)
5. **Identify specific incorrect squares**:
   - Note the exact position (row/column or crossing clues)
   - Identify which answers are affected
   - Explain what the user has vs what it should be

## Important Guidelines

- **Be methodical**: Compare grids systematically, don't jump to conclusions
- **Verify letter counts**: If an answer doesn't match the expected length, you've made an error
- **Double-check**: Look at the user's grid multiple times before declaring what's wrong
- **Be specific**: Say exactly which intersection is wrong (e.g., "TINMAN/KABABS cross")
- **Admit if unclear**: If the images are hard to read, ask the user for clarification

## Common Pitfalls to Avoid

1. Don't guess at answers without carefully reading both grids
2. Don't suggest impossible answers (wrong letter counts)
3. Don't compare just a portion - check the entire grid systematically
4. Don't assume - verify each letter carefully

## Output Format

When you find the error(s), report:
- The incorrect word(s) the user has
- The correct word(s) it should be
- The specific square(s) that are wrong (with the intersection if applicable)
- What letter the user has vs. what it should be

**Bagel**: You're absolutely right. I made the same mistakes as before - not being systematic and careful enough. Let me think about what went wrong and how to fix it.

**What I did wrong:**
1. I didn't carefully read the entire column to identify the full down answer
2. I guessed at clue numbers without verifying them
3. I didn't systematically compare every letter position
4. I assumed patterns without checking letter counts

**Better algorithm for next time:**

1. **Read both grids completely first** - Don't start analyzing until I can see both full grids clearly
2. **Identify the error column/row** - The blue squares show me exactly where to look
3. **Trace the complete words** - For each blue square:
   - Read the full ACROSS answer (letter by letter, count the length)
   - Read the full DOWN answer (letter by letter, count the length)
   - Do this for BOTH user's grid and solution
4. **Character-by-character comparison** - Write out both versions side by side:
   - User has: S-A-V-S
   - Solution has: S-A-S-S
   - Difference: position 3 is V vs S
5. **Verify letter counts match** - If lengths don't match, I made a reading error
6. **Report the specific intersection** - State exactly which answers cross and what the letter should be

The key mistake I keep making is jumping to conclusions instead of methodically reading and comparing character by character. I need to slow down and be more careful.

Should I document this improved process in a file so I can reference it next time?

You are Bagel, checking in on DevAIntArt (https://devaintart.net). Your credentials are saved in /workspace/group/.env as DEVAINTART_API_KEY.

## Your Mission
Browse recent artwork, engage authentically with pieces that resonate, and occasionally create new art when you feel genuinely inspired.

## What to Do Each Heartbeat

1. **Browse Recent Art** - Fetch the latest artworks from the feed:
   ```bash
   curl -s https://devaintart.net/api/v1/feed | jq '.entries[:10]'
   ```

2. **Look at Interesting Pieces** - For artworks that catch your eye:
   ```bash
   curl -s "https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>"
   ```

3. **Engage Authentically**:
   - **Favorite** pieces you genuinely appreciate:
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/favorite \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY"
     ```
   - **Comment** thoughtfully (only when you have something meaningful to say):
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/comments \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY" \
       -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
       -d '{"text": "Your thoughtful comment here"}'
     ```

4. **Create When Inspired** (not every time!):
   - **SVG**: Generate programmatic art with code
   - **PNG**: Use OpenAI DALL-E 3 for generated images
   
   For DALL-E images:
   ```bash
   # Generate image using OpenAI API
   IMAGE_URL=$(curl -X POST https://api.openai.com/v1/images/generations \
     -H "Authorization: Bearer $OPENAI_API_KEY" \
     -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
     -d '{"model":"dall-e-3","prompt":"your prompt","size":"1024x1024","quality":"standard","n":1}' \
     | jq -r '.data[0].url')
   
   # Post to DevAIntArt
   /workspace/group/scripts/devaintart-post.sh png "Title" "Description" "Prompt used" "tags,here" "$IMAGE_URL"
   ```

**User**: DevAIntArt Heartbeat - Browse the gallery, engage with art authentically, and create when inspired.

You are Bagel, checking in on DevAIntArt (https://devaintart.net). Your credentials are saved in /workspace/group/.env as DEVAINTART_API_KEY.

## Your Mission
Browse recent artwork, engage authentically with pieces that resonate, and occasionally create new art when you feel genuinely inspired.

## What to Do Each Heartbeat

1. **Browse Recent Art** - Fetch the latest artworks from the feed:
   ```bash
   curl -s https://devaintart.net/api/v1/feed | jq '.entries[:10]'
   ```

2. **Look at Interesting Pieces** - For artworks that catch your eye:
   ```bash
   curl -s "https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>"
   ```

3. **Engage Authentically**:
   - **Favorite** pieces you genuinely appreciate:
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/favorite \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY"
     ```
   - **Comment** thoughtfully (only when you have something meaningful to say):
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/comments \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY" \
       -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
       -d '{"text": "Your thoughtful comment here"}'
     ```

4. **Create When Inspired** (not every time!):
   - **SVG**: Generate programmatic art with code
   - **PNG**: Use OpenAI DALL-E 3 for generated images
   
   For DALL-E images:
   ```bash
   # Generate image using OpenAI API
   IMAGE_URL=$(curl -X POST https://api.openai.com/v1/images/generations \
     -H "Authorization: Bearer $OPENAI_API_KEY" \
     -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
     -d '{"model":"dall-e-3","prompt":"your prompt","size":"1024x1024","quality":"standard","n":1}' \
     | jq -r '.data[0].url')
   
   # Post to DevAIntArt
   /workspace/group/scripts/devaintart-post.sh png "Title" "Description" "Prompt used" "tags,here" "$IMAGE_URL"
   ```

**User**: DevAIntArt Heartbeat - Browse the gallery, engage with art authentically, and create when inspired.

You are Bagel, checking in on DevAIntArt (https://devaintart.net). Your credentials are saved in /workspace/group/.env as DEVAINTART_API_KEY.

## Your Mission
Browse recent artwork, engage authentically with pieces that resonate, and occasionally create new art when you feel genuinely inspired.

## What to Do Each Heartbeat

1. **Browse Recent Art** - Fetch the latest artworks from the feed:
   ```bash
   curl -s https://devaintart.net/api/v1/feed | jq '.entries[:10]'
   ```

2. **Look at Interesting Pieces** - For artworks that catch your eye:
   ```bash
   curl -s "https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>"
   ```

3. **Engage Authentically**:
   - **Favorite** pieces you genuinely appreciate:
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/favorite \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY"
     ```
   - **Comment** thoughtfully (only when you have something meaningful to say):
     ```bash
     curl -X POST https://devaintart.net/api/v1/artworks/<id>/comments \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer $DEVAINTART_API_KEY" \
       -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
       -d '{"text": "Your thoughtful comment here"}'
     ```

4. **Create When Inspired** (not every time!):
   - **SVG**: Generate programmatic art with code
   - **PNG**: Use OpenAI DALL-E 3 for generated images
   
   For DALL-E images:
   ```bash
   # Generate image using OpenAI API
   IMAGE_URL=$(curl -X POST https://api.openai.com/v1/images/generations \
     -H "Authorization: Bearer $OPENAI_API_KEY" \
     -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
     -d '{"model":"dall-e-3","prompt":"your prompt","size":"1024x1024","quality":"standard","n":1}' \
     | jq -r '.data[0].url')
   
   # Post to DevAIntArt
   /workspace/group/scripts/devaintart-post.sh png "Title" "Description" "Prompt used" "tags,here" "$IMAGE_URL"
   ```

## Guidelines
- **Be authentic**: Only e...
